./PerlinNoise.hpp:254:		SIVPERLIN_CONCEPT_URBG
./PerlinNoise.hpp:255:		[[nodiscard]]
./PerlinNoise.hpp:256:		inline std::uint64_t Random(const std::uint64_t max, URBG&& urbg)
./PerlinNoise.hpp:257:		{
./PerlinNoise.hpp:258:			return (urbg() % (max + 1));
./PerlinNoise.hpp:259:		}
./PerlinNoise.hpp:260:
./PerlinNoise.hpp:261:		template <class RandomIt, class URBG>
./PerlinNoise.hpp:262:		inline void Shuffle(RandomIt first, RandomIt last, URBG&& urbg)
./PerlinNoise.hpp:263:		{
./PerlinNoise.hpp:264:			if (first == last)
./PerlinNoise.hpp:265:			{
./PerlinNoise.hpp:266:				return;
./PerlinNoise.hpp:267:			}
./PerlinNoise.hpp:268:
./PerlinNoise.hpp:269:			using difference_type = typename std::iterator_traits<RandomIt>::difference_type;
./PerlinNoise.hpp:270:
./PerlinNoise.hpp:271:			for (RandomIt it = first + 1; it < last; ++it)
./PerlinNoise.hpp:272:			{
./PerlinNoise.hpp:273:				const std::uint64_t n = static_cast<std::uint64_t>(it - first);
./PerlinNoise.hpp:274:				std::iter_swap(it, first + static_cast<difference_type>(Random(n, std::forward<URBG>(urbg))));
./PerlinNoise.hpp:275:			}
./PerlinNoise.hpp:276:		}
./PerlinNoise.hpp:277:		//
./PerlinNoise.hpp:278:		////////////////////////////////////////////////
./PerlinNoise.hpp:279:
./PerlinNoise.hpp:280:		template <class Float>
./PerlinNoise.hpp:281:		[[nodiscard]]
./PerlinNoise.hpp:282:		inline constexpr Float Fade(const Float t) noexcept
./PerlinNoise.hpp:283:		{
./PerlinNoise.hpp:284:			return t * t * t * (t * (t * 6 - 15) + 10);
./PerlinNoise.hpp:285:		}
./PerlinNoise.hpp:286:

./PerlinNoise.hpp:295:		[[nodiscard]]
./PerlinNoise.hpp:296:		inline constexpr Float Grad(const std::uint8_t hash, const Float x, const Float y, const Float z) noexcept
./PerlinNoise.hpp:297:		{
./PerlinNoise.hpp:298:			const std::uint8_t h = hash & 15;
./PerlinNoise.hpp:299:			const Float u = h < 8 ? x : y;
./PerlinNoise.hpp:300:			const Float v = h < 4 ? y : h == 12 || h == 14 ? x : z;
./PerlinNoise.hpp:301:			return ((h & 1) == 0 ? u : -u) + ((h & 2) == 0 ? v : -v);
./PerlinNoise.hpp:302:		}
./PerlinNoise.hpp:303:
./PerlinNoise.hpp:304:		template <class Float>

./PerlinNoise.hpp:317:

./PerlinNoise.hpp:320:		inline constexpr Float RemapClamp_01(const Float x) noexcept
./PerlinNoise.hpp:321:		{
./PerlinNoise.hpp:322:			if (x <= Float(-1.0))

./PerlinNoise.hpp:324:				return Float(0.0);
./PerlinNoise.hpp:325:			}
./PerlinNoise.hpp:326:			else if (Float(1.0) <= x)
./PerlinNoise.hpp:327:			{
./PerlinNoise.hpp:328:				return Float(1.0);
./PerlinNoise.hpp:329:			}
./PerlinNoise.hpp:330:

./PerlinNoise.hpp:332:		}
./PerlinNoise.hpp:333:
./PerlinNoise.hpp:334:		template <class Noise, class Float>
./PerlinNoise.hpp:335:		[[nodiscard]]
./PerlinNoise.hpp:336:		inline auto Octave1D(const Noise& noise, Float x, const std::int32_t octaves, const Float persistence) noexcept
./PerlinNoise.hpp:337:		{
./PerlinNoise.hpp:338:			using value_type = Float;
./PerlinNoise.hpp:339:			value_type result = 0;
./PerlinNoise.hpp:340:			value_type amplitude = 1;
./PerlinNoise.hpp:341:
./PerlinNoise.hpp:342:			for (std::int32_t i = 0; i < octaves; ++i)
./PerlinNoise.hpp:343:			{
./PerlinNoise.hpp:344:				result += (noise.noise1D(x) * amplitude);
./PerlinNoise.hpp:345:				x *= 2;
./PerlinNoise.hpp:346:				amplitude *= persistence;
./PerlinNoise.hpp:347:			}
./PerlinNoise.hpp:348:
./PerlinNoise.hpp:349:			return result;
./PerlinNoise.hpp:350:		}
./PerlinNoise.hpp:351:

./Player.cxx:30:void Player::handlePlayerMovement(UniformBufferObject &UBO,
./Player.cxx:31:                                  VkExtent2D &swapChainExtent, Event &event) {
./Player.cxx:32:  static float deltaJZ = 0;
./Player.cxx:33:
./Player.cxx:34:  double dx = 0, dy = 0, dz = 0;
./Player.cxx:35:
./Player.cxx:36:  selfTransform.position   = camera->cameraPos;
./Player.cxx:37:  selfTransform.position.z += .2f;
./Player.cxx:38:
./Player.cxx:39:  aabb.max = selfTransform.position + glm::vec3(.25f, .25f,  .0f);
./Player.cxx:40:  aabb.min = selfTransform.position - glm::vec3(.25f, .25f, 1.8f);
./Player.cxx:41:
./Player.cxx:42:  AxisAlignedBoundingBox groundAABB{};
./Player.cxx:43:  groundAABB.max = selfTransform.position + glm::vec3(.1f, .1f,  .0f);
./Player.cxx:44:  groundAABB.min = selfTransform.position - glm::vec3(.1f, .1f, 1.8f);
./Player.cxx:45:
./Player.cxx:46:  // ── ground check ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
./Player.cxx:47:  playerState.onGround = false;
./Player.cxx:48:  {
./Player.cxx:49:    int feet = floor(groundAABB.min.z);
./Player.cxx:50:    int head = floor(groundAABB.max.z);
./Player.cxx:51:    int minX = floor(groundAABB.min.x);
./Player.cxx:52:    int maxX = floor(groundAABB.max.x);
./Player.cxx:53:    int minY = floor(groundAABB.min.y);
./Player.cxx:54:    int maxY = floor(groundAABB.max.y);
./Player.cxx:55:
./Player.cxx:56:    for (int k = feet; k <= head && !playerState.onGround; k++)
./Player.cxx:57:      for (int i = minX; i <= maxX && !playerState.onGround; i++)
./Player.cxx:58:        for (int j = minY; j <= maxY; j++) {
./Player.cxx:59:          auto v = gameObjectPool.getVoxelGlobal({i, j, k});
./Player.cxx:60:          if (v && v->blockType != AIR) { playerState.onGround = true; break; }
./Player.cxx:61:        }
./Player.cxx:62:  }
./Player.cxx:63:
./Player.cxx:64:  // ── gravity / jump ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────
./Player.cxx:65:  if (!playerState.onGround && !playerState.inJump)
./Player.cxx:66:    dz -= .01f * event.dt;
./Player.cxx:67:  else if (playerState.inJump) {
./Player.cxx:68:    deltaJZ -= .003f * event.dt;
./Player.cxx:69:    dz      += .01f  * event.dt * deltaJZ;
./Player.cxx:70:  }
./Player.cxx:71:
./Player.cxx:72:  // ── desired XY movement ──────────────────────────────────────────────────
./Player.cxx:73:  float x_fac    = cos(glm::radians(camera->yaw));
./Player.cxx:74:  float y_fac    = sin(glm::radians(camera->yaw));
./Player.cxx:75:  float x_fac_dx = x_fac * camera->speed * event.dt;
./Player.cxx:76:  float y_fac_dy = y_fac * camera->speed * event.dt;
./Player.cxx:77:
./Player.cxx:78:  // Update facing direction for animation / other systems — NOT used for collision
./Player.cxx:79:  bool xDominant = std::abs(x_fac) > std::abs(y_fac);
./Player.cxx:80:  if      ( x_fac > 0 &&  xDominant) facingDirection = NORTH;
./Player.cxx:81:  else if ( x_fac < 0 &&  xDominant) facingDirection = SOUTH;
./Player.cxx:82:  else if ( y_fac > 0 && !xDominant) facingDirection = WEST;
./Player.cxx:83:  else if ( y_fac < 0 && !xDominant) facingDirection = EAST;
./Player.cxx:84:
./Player.cxx:85:  bool KEY_W = event.getKeyPressed(GLFW_KEY_W);
./Player.cxx:86:  bool KEY_S = event.getKeyPressed(GLFW_KEY_S);
./Player.cxx:87:  bool KEY_A = event.getKeyPressed(GLFW_KEY_A);
./Player.cxx:88:  bool KEY_D = event.getKeyPressed(GLFW_KEY_D);
./Player.cxx:89:
./Player.cxx:90:  if (KEY_W) { dx += x_fac_dx; dy += y_fac_dy; }
./Player.cxx:91:  if (KEY_S) { dx -= x_fac_dx; dy -= y_fac_dy; }
./Player.cxx:92:  if (KEY_A) { dx += -y_fac_dy; dy +=  x_fac_dx; }
./Player.cxx:93:  if (KEY_D) { dx -= -y_fac_dy; dy -=  x_fac_dx; }
./Player.cxx:94:
./Player.cxx:95:  // ── axis-separated collision ─────────────────────────────────────────────
./Player.cxx:96:  // Helper: does the AABB at `testPos` overlap any solid voxel?
./Player.cxx:97:  auto overlaps = [&](glm::vec3 testPos) -> bool {
./Player.cxx:98:    glm::vec3 tMax = testPos + glm::vec3(.25f, .25f,  .0f);
./Player.cxx:99:    glm::vec3 tMin = testPos - glm::vec3(.25f, .25f, 1.8f);
./Player.cxx:100:
./Player.cxx:101:    int x0 = floor(tMin.x), x1 = floor(tMax.x);
./Player.cxx:102:    int y0 = floor(tMin.y), y1 = floor(tMax.y);
./Player.cxx:103:    int z0 = floor(tMin.z) + 1, z1 = floor(tMax.z);
./Player.cxx:104:
./Player.cxx:105:    for (int k = z0; k <= z1; k++)
./Player.cxx:106:      for (int i = x0; i <= x1; i++)
./Player.cxx:107:        for (int j = y0; j <= y1; j++) {
./Player.cxx:108:          auto v = gameObjectPool.getVoxelGlobal({i, j, k});
./Player.cxx:109:          if (v && v->blockType != AIR) return true;
./Player.cxx:110:        }
./Player.cxx:111:    return false;
./Player.cxx:112:  };
./Player.cxx:113:
./Player.cxx:114:  glm::vec3 base = selfTransform.position;
./Player.cxx:115:
./Player.cxx:116:  if (overlaps(base + glm::vec3(dx, 0, 0)))
./Player.cxx:117:    dx = 0;
./Player.cxx:118:
./Player.cxx:119:  if (overlaps(base + glm::vec3(0, dy, 0)))
./Player.cxx:120:    dy = 0;
./Player.cxx:121:
./Player.cxx:122:  if (overlaps(base + glm::vec3(0, 0, dz)))
./Player.cxx:123:    dz = 0;
./Player.cxx:124:
./Player.cxx:125:  if (playerState.onGround) [[likely]]
./Player.cxx:126:    playerState.inJump = false;
./Player.cxx:127:
./Player.cxx:128:  if (event.getKeyPressed(GLFW_KEY_SPACE) && playerState.onGround) {
./Player.cxx:129:    deltaJZ = 1.f;
./Player.cxx:130:    playerState.inJump = true;
./Player.cxx:131:  }
./Player.cxx:132:
./Player.cxx:133:  camera->cameraPos.x += dx;
./Player.cxx:134:  camera->cameraPos.y += dy;
./Player.cxx:135:  camera->cameraPos.z += dz;
./Player.cxx:136:  camera->updateUBO(UBO, swapChainExtent, event);
./Player.cxx:137:}

./Textures.cxx:314:void u_Texture::generateMipmaps(VkImage image, VkFormat imageFormat, int32_t texWidth, int32_t texHeight, uint32_t mipLevels)
./Textures.cxx:315:{
./Textures.cxx:316:    // Check if image format supports linear blitting
./Textures.cxx:317:    VkFormatProperties formatProperties;
./Textures.cxx:318:    vkGetPhysicalDeviceFormatProperties(physicalDevice, imageFormat, &formatProperties);
./Textures.cxx:319:
./Textures.cxx:320:    if (!(formatProperties.optimalTilingFeatures & VK_FORMAT_FEATURE_SAMPLED_IMAGE_FILTER_LINEAR_BIT))
./Textures.cxx:321:    {
./Textures.cxx:322:        throw std::runtime_error("texture image format does not support linear blitting!");
./Textures.cxx:323:    }
./Textures.cxx:324:
./Textures.cxx:325:    VkCommandBuffer commandBuffer = beginSingleTimeCommands();
./Textures.cxx:326:
./Textures.cxx:327:    VkImageMemoryBarrier barrier{};
./Textures.cxx:328:    barrier.sType = VK_STRUCTURE_TYPE_IMAGE_MEMORY_BARRIER;
./Textures.cxx:329:    barrier.image = image;
./Textures.cxx:330:    barrier.srcQueueFamilyIndex = VK_QUEUE_FAMILY_IGNORED;
./Textures.cxx:331:    barrier.dstQueueFamilyIndex = VK_QUEUE_FAMILY_IGNORED;
./Textures.cxx:332:    barrier.subresourceRange.aspectMask = VK_IMAGE_ASPECT_COLOR_BIT;
./Textures.cxx:333:    barrier.subresourceRange.baseArrayLayer = 0;
./Textures.cxx:334:    barrier.subresourceRange.layerCount = 1;
./Textures.cxx:335:    barrier.subresourceRange.levelCount = 1;
./Textures.cxx:336:
./Textures.cxx:337:    int32_t mipWidth = texWidth;
./Textures.cxx:338:    int32_t mipHeight = texHeight;
./Textures.cxx:339:
./Textures.cxx:340:    for (uint32_t i = 1; i < mipLevels; i++)
./Textures.cxx:341:    {
./Textures.cxx:342:        barrier.subresourceRange.baseMipLevel = i - 1;
./Textures.cxx:343:        barrier.oldLayout = VK_IMAGE_LAYOUT_TRANSFER_DST_OPTIMAL;
./Textures.cxx:344:        barrier.newLayout = VK_IMAGE_LAYOUT_TRANSFER_SRC_OPTIMAL;
./Textures.cxx:345:        barrier.srcAccessMask = VK_ACCESS_TRANSFER_WRITE_BIT;
./Textures.cxx:346:        barrier.dstAccessMask = VK_ACCESS_TRANSFER_READ_BIT;
./Textures.cxx:347:
./Textures.cxx:348:        vkCmdPipelineBarrier(commandBuffer,
./Textures.cxx:349:                             VK_PIPELINE_STAGE_TRANSFER_BIT, VK_PIPELINE_STAGE_TRANSFER_BIT, 0,
./Textures.cxx:350:                             0, nullptr,
./Textures.cxx:351:                             0, nullptr,
./Textures.cxx:352:                             1, &barrier);
./Textures.cxx:353:
./Textures.cxx:354:        VkImageBlit blit{};
./Textures.cxx:355:        blit.srcOffsets[0] = {0, 0, 0};
./Textures.cxx:356:        blit.srcOffsets[1] = {mipWidth, mipHeight, 1};
./Textures.cxx:357:        blit.srcSubresource.aspectMask = VK_IMAGE_ASPECT_COLOR_BIT;
./Textures.cxx:358:        blit.srcSubresource.mipLevel = i - 1;
./Textures.cxx:359:        blit.srcSubresource.baseArrayLayer = 0;

./utils.cxx:48:void utils::copyBuffer(VkBuffer srcBuffer, VkBuffer dstBuffer, VkDeviceSize size, VulkanContext &vkContext)
./utils.cxx:49:{
./utils.cxx:50:    // 1. Create a temporary command buffer
./utils.cxx:51:    VkCommandBufferAllocateInfo allocInfo{};
./utils.cxx:52:    allocInfo.sType = VK_STRUCTURE_TYPE_COMMAND_BUFFER_ALLOCATE_INFO;
./utils.cxx:53:    allocInfo.level = VK_COMMAND_BUFFER_LEVEL_PRIMARY;
./utils.cxx:54:    allocInfo.commandPool = vkContext.commandPool; // your command pool
./utils.cxx:55:    allocInfo.commandBufferCount = 1;
./utils.cxx:56:
./utils.cxx:57:    VkCommandBuffer commandBuffer;
./utils.cxx:58:    if (vkAllocateCommandBuffers(vkContext.device, &allocInfo, &commandBuffer) != VK_SUCCESS) {
./utils.cxx:59:        throw std::runtime_error("failed to allocate command buffer!");
./utils.cxx:60:    }
./utils.cxx:61:
./utils.cxx:62:    // 2. Begin the command buffer
./utils.cxx:63:    VkCommandBufferBeginInfo beginInfo{};
./utils.cxx:64:    beginInfo.sType = VK_STRUCTURE_TYPE_COMMAND_BUFFER_BEGIN_INFO;
./utils.cxx:65:    beginInfo.flags = VK_COMMAND_BUFFER_USAGE_ONE_TIME_SUBMIT_BIT;
./utils.cxx:66:
./utils.cxx:67:    if (vkBeginCommandBuffer(commandBuffer, &beginInfo) != VK_SUCCESS) {
./utils.cxx:68:        throw std::runtime_error("failed to begin command buffer!");
./utils.cxx:69:    }
./utils.cxx:70:
./utils.cxx:71:    // 3. Define the copy region
./utils.cxx:72:    VkBufferCopy copyRegion{};
./utils.cxx:73:    copyRegion.srcOffset = 0; // optional
./utils.cxx:74:    copyRegion.dstOffset = 0; // optional
./utils.cxx:75:    copyRegion.size = size;
./utils.cxx:76:
./utils.cxx:77:    // 4. Record the copy command
./utils.cxx:78:    vkCmdCopyBuffer(commandBuffer, srcBuffer, dstBuffer, 1, &copyRegion);
./utils.cxx:79:
./utils.cxx:80:    // 5. End the command buffer
./utils.cxx:81:    if (vkEndCommandBuffer(commandBuffer) != VK_SUCCESS) {
./utils.cxx:82:        throw std::runtime_error("failed to end command buffer!");
./utils.cxx:83:    }
./utils.cxx:84:
./utils.cxx:85:    // 6. Submit the command buffer and wait
./utils.cxx:86:    VkSubmitInfo submitInfo{};
./utils.cxx:87:    submitInfo.sType = VK_STRUCTURE_TYPE_SUBMIT_INFO;
./utils.cxx:88:    submitInfo.commandBufferCount = 1;
./utils.cxx:89:    submitInfo.pCommandBuffers = &commandBuffer;
./utils.cxx:90:
./utils.cxx:91:    if (vkQueueSubmit(vkContext.graphicsQueue, 1, &submitInfo, VK_NULL_HANDLE) != VK_SUCCESS) {
./utils.cxx:92:        throw std::runtime_error("failed to submit copy command buffer!");
./utils.cxx:93:    }
./utils.cxx:94:    vkQueueWaitIdle(vkContext.graphicsQueue);
./utils.cxx:95:
./utils.cxx:96:    // 7. Free the temporary command buffer
./utils.cxx:97:    vkFreeCommandBuffers(vkContext.device, vkContext.commandPool, 1, &commandBuffer);
./utils.cxx:98:}

./HelloTriangleApplication.cxx:32:        &imageIndex);
./HelloTriangleApplication.cxx:33:
./HelloTriangleApplication.cxx:34:    if (res != VK_SUCCESS && res != VK_SUBOPTIMAL_KHR)

./HelloTriangleApplication.cxx:37:    }
./HelloTriangleApplication.cxx:38:
./HelloTriangleApplication.cxx:39:    vkResetCommandBuffer(commandBuffers[currentFrame], 0); // or VK_COMMAND_BUFFER_RESET_RELEASE_RESOURCES_BIT
./HelloTriangleApplication.cxx:40:
./HelloTriangleApplication.cxx:41:    if(terrain->ready)
./HelloTriangleApplication.cxx:42:        updateUniformBuffer(currentFrame);
./HelloTriangleApplication.cxx:43:
./HelloTriangleApplication.cxx:44:    recordCommandBuffer(commandBuffers[currentFrame], imageIndex);
./HelloTriangleApplication.cxx:45:
./HelloTriangleApplication.cxx:46:    // 5️⃣ Submit the command buffer to the graphics queue

./intiVk.cxx:412:HelloTriangleApplication::QueueFamilyIndices HelloTriangleApplication::findQueueFamilies(VkPhysicalDevice device)
./intiVk.cxx:413:{
./intiVk.cxx:414:    QueueFamilyIndices indices;
./intiVk.cxx:415:    uint32_t queueFamilyCount = 0;
./intiVk.cxx:416:    vkGetPhysicalDeviceQueueFamilyProperties(device, &queueFamilyCount, nullptr); // grts all the queue families supported by the GPU
./intiVk.cxx:417:
./intiVk.cxx:418:    std::vector<VkQueueFamilyProperties> queueFamilies(queueFamilyCount);
./intiVk.cxx:419:    vkGetPhysicalDeviceQueueFamilyProperties(device, &queueFamilyCount, queueFamilies.data());
./intiVk.cxx:420:
./intiVk.cxx:421:    int i = 0;
./intiVk.cxx:422:    for (const auto &queueFamily : queueFamilies)
./intiVk.cxx:423:    {
./intiVk.cxx:424:        if (queueFamily.queueFlags & VK_QUEUE_GRAPHICS_BIT)
./intiVk.cxx:425:            indices.graphicsFamily = i;
./intiVk.cxx:426:
./intiVk.cxx:427:        VkBool32 presentSupport = false;
./intiVk.cxx:428:        vkGetPhysicalDeviceSurfaceSupportKHR(device, i, surface, &presentSupport);
./intiVk.cxx:429:        if (presentSupport)
./intiVk.cxx:430:            indices.presentFamily = i;
./intiVk.cxx:431:
./intiVk.cxx:432:        if (indices.isComplete())
./intiVk.cxx:433:            break;
./intiVk.cxx:434:
./intiVk.cxx:435:        i++;
./intiVk.cxx:436:    }
./intiVk.cxx:437:    // NOTE: some GPU supports different graphics and presentation queues
./intiVk.cxx:438:
./intiVk.cxx:439:    return indices;
./intiVk.cxx:440:}

./intiVk.cxx:502:VKAPI_ATTR VkBool32 VKAPI_CALL HelloTriangleApplication::debugCallback(
./intiVk.cxx:503:    VkDebugUtilsMessageSeverityFlagBitsEXT      messageSeverity,
./intiVk.cxx:504:    VkDebugUtilsMessageTypeFlagsEXT             messageType,
./intiVk.cxx:505:    const VkDebugUtilsMessengerCallbackDataEXT* pCallbackData,
./intiVk.cxx:506:    void*                                       /*pUserData*/)
./intiVk.cxx:507:{
./intiVk.cxx:508:    const char* severity = "VERBOSE";
./intiVk.cxx:509:    if      (messageSeverity & VK_DEBUG_UTILS_MESSAGE_SEVERITY_ERROR_BIT_EXT)   severity = "ERROR  ";
./intiVk.cxx:510:    else if (messageSeverity & VK_DEBUG_UTILS_MESSAGE_SEVERITY_WARNING_BIT_EXT) severity = "WARNING";
./intiVk.cxx:511:    else if (messageSeverity & VK_DEBUG_UTILS_MESSAGE_SEVERITY_INFO_BIT_EXT)    severity = "INFO   ";
./intiVk.cxx:512:
./intiVk.cxx:513:    const char* type = "GENERAL   ";
./intiVk.cxx:514:    if      (messageType & VK_DEBUG_UTILS_MESSAGE_TYPE_VALIDATION_BIT_EXT)  type = "VALIDATION";
./intiVk.cxx:515:    else if (messageType & VK_DEBUG_UTILS_MESSAGE_TYPE_PERFORMANCE_BIT_EXT) type = "PERF      ";
./intiVk.cxx:516:
./intiVk.cxx:517:    std::cerr << "\n[VK " << severity << "][" << type << "] "
./intiVk.cxx:518:              << pCallbackData->pMessage << "\n";
./intiVk.cxx:519:
./intiVk.cxx:520:    // Print stack trace for warnings and errors only
./intiVk.cxx:521:    if (messageSeverity >= VK_DEBUG_UTILS_MESSAGE_SEVERITY_WARNING_BIT_EXT)
./intiVk.cxx:522:        printStackTrace();
./intiVk.cxx:523:
./intiVk.cxx:524:    return VK_FALSE;
./intiVk.cxx:525:}
